梅琪伊文斯所說她不願做女明星的理由（下）  新尼　　「我亦常常這樣想，如果我僅僅做了一位女領導人，我所得的報酬，比做一位明星還多。譬如說，一個女演員被人家轟了起來，做了一個明星，她立卽魷被人認成某一作風的角色（　）。她的作風一旦被大衆所認定之後，就不能再變動了。她雖然一心一意的想扮演別種的角色，但是已經再沒有希望的了。　　當一個電影脚本送進了公司之後，公司的頭腦略爲看了一看，魷說：『這齣悲對於某某，是再好沒有的了。她那種悲傷的表演，楚人人喜歡看的。』他們或者說：『這種鄉村的羅曼斯，是不合於某某的作風的。退回去。她不能扮演農家女子的。她的觀衆看了，都會從戲院裏走出去的。』　　公司的當局亦沒有法子，他們祇好惟觀衆之意楚從。所以一個女明星，在第一次扮演一種角色成名之後，就得永遠的扮演那個角色，直到她老了，或是觀衆們看厭了爲止。女領導人，或是特別演員，却是運氣好些，她不至於被列爲某一種類，而失去其他表演的機會。　　再則每一個未婚的女子，都有些羅曼諦克的夢想，要想會見她理想中的人情的。我現在做了特別演員就可以常常和千萬女子所崇拜的男明星會見。我差不多和所有的男明星，都合演過戲。和一般的普通女子一樣，當我和克拉克蓋博，羅勃蒙高茂萊，或是雷門諾伐羅合拍電影的時候，我就覺得非常的偷快。我到了好萊塢，已經有三年之久，而這次我才得到一些假期。因此這三年以來忽忙之中，我已經和多少男明星合拍過戲，亦就可想而知了。倘使我做了一個明星，我就沒有這許多好機會了。　　我們做演員的，在表演的小動作上面，總有一種別的形態，而觀衆們在看戲的時候，就不知不覺的希望看到那些小動作的流露出來。所以我們有影戲的時候，常常聽見旁座的人說：『他怯要從耳　了』，或是『她快要低下睫毛，口微微顫動，表示失望了。』這種預測，在老於看戲的影迷，十次之中有九次是猜得中的。我覺得一個明星的小動作，變成了刻板式，是很危險的。是自已常常審查我的動作，我面部的表情，不讓我自己成功一種呆板的習慣。但是我因爲不是一個明星，可以時常扮演着各色各樣的角色，於我小動作方面的變化，是有了極大的帮助。　　我還有一個理由，使我不願意做一個明星。常明我拍攝「塊肉餘生」的時候，我嘗到了異樣的與趣。我常常站在攝影塲中，看許多大藝太家的表演。那裏有里昂巴里穆亞，愛娜梅奧立芙，肯勃爾古柏，弗蘭克勞頓，華德　爾資等。我看了他們表演的神乎其技，我就覺得我應該怎樣的刻苦學習，才可以好這些大藝術領袖，同站在一個平等的地位。　　那不單單在一頭的金黃頭髮一副秀麗的眉目，一個苗條的身段，或是怎樣的誘惑力。要做一等的明星，需要多年的刻苦工作。她的神經系統，應當是橡皮做的，好被擊下一百萬次，一百萬次的反躍起來。此外她還要有些天才，好在你已經獲得了一等地位之後，能自已維持下去。　　我因爲年紀還輕，所以有很大的抱負。但是我亦不是小孩子，應當自己知道自己的限制。並且我的常識，告訴我要脚踏實地。我沒有什麽動會處。在這一點，見仁貝智。自然觀念不同，但我却自以爲幸。我亦不能算美麗，聰明，具有異樣情調，或有驚人之處。我亦沒有學過跳舞，唱歌，彫刻或油畫。我不過楚一個以在銀幕上表演的職業的女子。但我在攝影塲之外，我可以忘記，我是個女演員。我可以逍遙自在，無拘無束。那就因爲我不是一個明星的原故。」（完）影片談評評「孤島飄流記」  繼漢　　Menor　Aran—國泰　　被改譯作「孤島飄流記」的名作「亞倫島的人們」是記錄影片。　　關於記錄影片，以前也曾看過記錄天文的，但却一時記不起那影片的名字，雖然它也曾給與我一個深的印象。同時我也記得那一部作品並沒有拋粱故事的結構，並不像這一影片完全沒有故事的形式。在這裏似乎有「記錄影片」是否應當有故事？—這一問題頗值得研究一下　　當觀衆從鑒賞習慣上，不能在無故事的影片中得着滿足的時候，有故事的記錄影片，是更足以增加鑒賞者的興趣。即如范達克的「愛斯基摩」，假使也是記錄影片的話，那末他是成功了的。他將愛斯基摩的人們的生活，習慣，以及他們和大自然戰鬥，描畫他們在白種人的欺騙，與詐取之下所遭受着種慘遇，以後者爲故事的綫索，再以前者的種種編織在故事中間。但是「愛斯基摩」，人們不會將它歸入記錄影片一類。而前面說到那天象記錄的影片，却又因着故事的着重，使「記錄」本身反而成爲附屬的穿挿。　　記錄影片在蘇聯是作爲重要的課題，被研究與實踐着，如會經在新光開映「莫斯科之朝」便是好例。那兒完全沒有故事的形式，作者充分的使用音樂的Tempo將片斷的新聞片織接起來。但是一部短片，比較容易獲得效果些，至少觀衆們是不會因之厭頃的。　　現在我們又看到這一部沒有故事作中心的「亞倫島的人們」了，這是八千呎以上的長片。大概看過這一影片的人們，特別是要求曲折離奇，悲歡離合的劇情的人們，對於這一影片不會十分滿足的，而且會因着對於單調而感覺枯澀。這不能不是一般共同的感覺。這樣說來，未嘗不是作品在效果上的損失。　　現在我們來看這一影片所表現着的一切罷。再明顯沒有的，作者告訴我們人類爲了生存，得以大無畏的精神，繼續不斷的無休止的和大自然爭鬥。在這亞倫島上的居民，他們沒有樹木，沒有可以種植的土地，因之他們的生存，必需以海藻和岩石縫中的碎土，作爲種植馬鈴薯之用。當他們在採土的時候，他們是那般珍惜不肯拋棄很少的一撮。此外他們的日常生活，便是捕魚，小的魚固然易於到手，而大的莎魚，他們是日以繼夜的捕打着。在海面平靜的時候，海鷗在飢餓的飛翔哀鳴，他們的工作似乎比較容易一些，可是當海中風濤澎湃的時候，他們是拚着性命和大海搏鬥。他們不能戰勝波濤，便得給大海吞沒。他們的生活戰鬥，永遠沒有實止，除非他們給大海吞噬了以致於可怕的休止。　　是的，在這裏表現着人生是何等艱難，你不搏鬥，你就得死。這裹是人類和大自然的搏鬥，而人與人之間的搏鬥，更是何等可怕和殘酷啊！這裏是一首粗獷沉重的詩化的戰鬥呼號聲，這沉重的詩啊，不是謳歌人生，也不是爲悲慘的命運而惋悄，它是戰鬥的吶喊與呼號。它不使話笑，也不使你哭，它只使你體念着人生的意義，沉重的向前邁進。　　是的，這裏楚詩，也是一幅雄偉的黑白分明的祖綫條的木刻，圖畫。假使我們不是盲目者，我們不能不爲這繪畫而感動，不能不對這美麗的攝影大聲讚美。作者羅伯脫林萊赫迭（Robert　Flaherty）他是那樣靈活的處理鏡頭的角度，他對於音響效果也是有機的發揮了獨立的效能，同時在剪接上也是有着優越的成績。　　「春風秋雨」中之一幕（克勞黛　爾白主演）「肝腸寸裂的母親！」南京映電影小說小牧師（Little　Minister）（三）  志　　當巴白娜將到古堡時，她發現防守的哨兵了。她知道她自己一身的吉普西衣服不能通過去的。這時恰巧給她拾到了一件披肩。她正想披着冒險衝過去的時候，却望見覺民從古堡的小路走過來。她就跑出來站在他的旁邊，手勾住了他的臂。當然，覺民一身的牧師衣裳，是毫無困難地給他們通過了。因爲兵十們誤會她楚覺民的妻子。覺民想辯護，却給她用說話阻擋了。她的俏皮，眞把他弄得沒法。　　他們行近了收師的往宅了。裏面還有燈光。覺的說道：「這就是我的住宅。那是我母親房間裏的燈光。」「祗有你的母親嗎？」她問。「祇有，如果你給人家捉着了，那麼人人都知道我是認你作妻子把你放走的。我不是怕人家妁責罰，我是怕良心上的痛苦呢。我的母親你　不曉得。她愛着我，相信着我，指導着我。我現在的有今日，她眞是快活極了。但是倘若今晚的事悄給人家知道了，我的敎會就會把我驅逐出來的。「他說完了，巴白娜就回頭向有兵士的路上去。「你往那裏去？」他隨後呌着。「我去自首去，但你不嬰驚，我不會連累你的。」「不，不要這樣。你等在花園裏，等到路通了再走吧。巴白娜滿腔含淚的說道：「你是好人，我很歡喜你。」可是他驚惶地急着道：「不要這樣說，你在那邊的屋子裏坐着等吧」。　　她坐在花園裏等。她看見房子裏的燈光熄滅。她心裏在幻想他們母子的生活。她覺得他們的生活是她的新經歷。今天早晨，她所思想的衹有她自己的一切。但現在她却認識了一個人，而這個人是完全爲別人服務的。　　有一次她又看見他了。他是去探望一位老婦蘭莉。因爲蘭莉沒有錢，而要被送入養老院了。他來勤慰她。巴白娜剛巧走了來，蘭莉的苦處，感動了她的惻隱之心。她答應供給她錢。使她仍然得住在這裏。這樣一來，她就想到了法子，每個星期都可以和小牧師會面。因爲她答應了小牧師，每星期給錢請他拿去送給蘭莉。覺民不得不答應了她。那時的蘭莉，感激得流着淚謝道：「謝謝你小姐。從此我就可以安心了。我希望你也是永遠的安樂。」巴白娜傷心地答道：「我的命還是不會安樂的了。」說完，就道着晚安走了。覺民也跟着出來說道：「「我希望你的命運不會不安的。」巴白娜忙問道：「你眞的擔心我的事囑？」「眞的，」他誠摯地說。「這是因爲你不了解我。」「這是因爲我了解你。」巴白娜答着道：「你認識了我還不久呢。」「巴白娜」，覺民呌着她，可是她却逃跑了。　　當她們在紗廠見面的時候，巴白娜本來是立意不多講話的，但是人非木石，何况是多悄善感的她呢。每個星期，他們都會面。每一次見着他，巴白娜都說這是最後的一次，但是她却每一次都去。等到有一次他抱着她誠懇地向她說道：「巴白娜，你就是我的主宰，我的一切。」她明白他的確是了解她而愛她了。她快活地唱着歌，在嘉定林裏跑回家。她不願意嫁給公爵了。但是你件事不會這樣的簡單。巴白娜是受着村人們崎視的，而小牧師又有這麽多的村人監視着。她雖然知道有人常看見他們在一起，但她却不理會這對於他的名譽是有影響的。（未完）

1935.04.18

Resolutions of the Central Political Council: Commendation for Meritorious Service in Closing the Breach, Convening a National Judicial Conference, and Approval for Fujian to Issue Two Types of Provincial Bonds 1

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council convened its 533rd meeting at 9:00 AM on the 17th, concerning prior conditions of the Fourth Water Conservancy Committee. Attendees included Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Ye Chucang, Yu Youren, Lin Sen, Kong Xiangxi, Ma Chaojun, Chu Minyi, Zhu Jiahua, and over thirty others. The meeting was chaired by Ye Chucang, and the resolutions reached are as follows:

(1) The closure of the breach in the Yellow River at Guantai should be investigated by the National Government to ascertain the meritorious service of Kong Xiangrong and other contributing personnel, who should be commended accordingly. Furthermore, the provincial governments along the river should be instructed to provide swift relief to the disaster victims.

(2) The request from the Judicial Yuan to convene a National Judicial Conference and the conference regulations were approved for record.

(3) The principles of the regulations for two types of bonds to be issued by the Fujian Provincial Government were approved with revisions and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. These include a 3 million yuan local construction public bond for the 24th year of the Republic of China and a 5 million yuan bond for settling old debts.

(4) Wu Zhongxin was appointed as a member and chairman of the Guizhou Provincial Government. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Nanjing) The closure of the breach at the Guantai mouth of the Yellow River was completed on the morning of the 11th. Kong Xiangxi reported to the Central Political Council on the 17th regarding the difficult process of closure and dike construction. The original report was lengthy, detailing (1) the efforts to build dikes after the breach the year before last, (2) the reasons for the breach again after the closure of the Changyuan mouth last year, (3) the negligence and delays of the river work personnel of the Labor-Relief Group before its transfer to the Economic Commission, leading to a precarious situation,

(4) the Economic Commission's efforts to remedy the situation, resulting in a successful closure. The report was very detailed and stated that the harm of the Yellow River's water flow lies not only in its excessive volume but also in its excessive sediment content, which settles and shifts constantly. The downstream riverbed has been rising for years, causing poor drainage and more frequent breaches, making closure more difficult. He instructed Li Yizhi, the chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, to quickly repair and reinforce the Jin堤 (Jin Di) before the major flood season. He also telegraphed the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission and the provincial governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, noting that the dikes of the three provinces had been in disrepair for many years, and requested them to plan and cooperate on the repair and defense of the dikes in the three provinces as soon as possible. He also suggested inviting Chinese and foreign experts to conduct thorough research so that the Yellow River disaster could be reduced and the lives and property of those along the river could be protected. The report concluded by stating that a telegram had recently been received from the supervisory committee sent by the Control Yuan, stating that the closure at Guantai was excellent and that continued efforts were needed to increase its height and thickness to achieve complete success. The rapid closure was due to sufficient funding and unified authority, which resulted in twice the result with half the effort. Regarding the construction funds, Kong Xiangxi allocated 450,000 yuan after Director Kong Xiangrong took over the remedial project. After the project is completed, the director will be responsible for submitting the expenses for reimbursement to respect public funds. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Zhang Xueliang Flies Back to Hubei 2

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang returned to Hubei from Chongqing on the 17th. The plane landed at the airport at 3:30 PM. Qian Dajun and others, having heard the news beforehand, were all there to greet him. Zhang immediately went to the headquarters to handle official business. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Chongqing) Zhang Xueliang, accompanied by his advisor Donald, flew to Hankou on a Kangning aircraft on the afternoon of the 17th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Hankou) Zhang Jiluan, the chief editor of the Tianjin Dagongbao, and another person arrived in Chongqing by plane from Guizhou on the 16th and flew to Hankou by plane on the 17th, arriving in the afternoon. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang returned here by plane from Guiyang this afternoon. Zhang, accompanied by his advisor Donald, planned to fly to Guizhou Province on Monday, but due to poor weather and poor visibility, the plane was forced to return, nearly falling into the Communist-controlled area. Fortunately, the pilot was skilled and averted disaster. According to Zhang, he saw many Communists marching west through the window of the plane, seemingly attempting to flee to Yunnan Province. At that time, a team of government troops rushed to intercept them. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

Sichuan Army Captures Langzhong City 3

(Chongqing) Military news: Our Peng Brigade moved out from Laoya Rock on the morning of the 15th, defeating the enemy, the 79th and 81st Regiments of the Pseudo-Ninth Army, in front of them. At noon, they reached Nanjin Pass. The enemy retreated towards the Bamiao A方向 (Bamiao A Fangxiang). All the pontoon boats were burned. Our army immediately sent a team to cross the river and occupied Langzhong City. Most of the enemy and major organs were stationed at Jinxian Chang and Mianyang. A telegram from the front stated that our army occupied Meizi A on the 15th. The enemy retreated towards Lingxi Temple Hongtu Pass. They are now crossing the river to attack. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

(Chongqing) The Communists in Shu Province attempted to seize Jiangyou but failed and retreated to the east bank of the Fu River. They encountered the Fifth Route Army on Monday and were subjected to a fierce attack by infantry and aircraft, suffering heavy casualties. The Communists are now west of the Fu River and the Jialing River, surrounded by troops on all sides, making it difficult for them to flee elsewhere. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

National Government Announces Regulations for the Pacification Commissioner's Office in Guizhou, Establishing a Special Commissioner to Handle Pacification Affairs, Dividing the Area into Several Districts, Each with a District Commander 4

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 17th announcing the organizational regulations of the Pacification Commissioner's Office in Guizhou, totaling eight articles. The main points are: (1) To handle pacification affairs in Guizhou Province and adjacent border areas, a Pacification Commissioner's Office is established with a Pacification Commissioner in Guizhou presiding over it; (2) The duties of the Pacification Commissioner are as follows: 1. Command the troops and local militias within the district to eliminate the remaining bandits in the area; 2. Supervise and guide the education of the troops and local militias within the district, as well as the organization and training of the populace; 3. Complete military-related transportation within the district; 4. Handle post-banditry affairs in the bandit-affected areas; 5. Provide relief to refugees; (3) Based on the conditions in Guizhou Province and adjacent border areas, the Pacification Commissioner's Office will divide the area under its jurisdiction into several districts, with the commander of the troops stationed in each district serving as the district commander, who will manage the affairs within the district under the direction of the Pacification Commissioner; the boundaries of each district will be determined separately; (4) The Pacification Commissioner may issue temporary commands to the pacification districts and county governments and other political and military organs under its jurisdiction for the implementation of pacification; (5) The Pacification Commissioner shall consult with the provincial party headquarters and the provincial government on party and government affairs related to pacification within the district. (Central News Agency dispatch, 17th)

Bandit Puppet Regiment Commander Defects, Bandit Leader Mao Zedong Severely Ill, Puppet Chief of Staff Killed in Bombing 5

(Changsha) Fan Zhuzhong, the commander of a puppet regiment of bandits who had been harassing Guidong, defected with his weapons, leading 19 bandits and surrendering 15 rifles. (Central News Agency dispatch, 16th)

(Changsha) Telegraph from He: The bandit Mao Zedong is severely ill, and the bandits are carrying him away as they flee. Also, Liu Bocheng, the puppet chief of staff of the bandit forces, was killed by our bombing. The remaining bandits are fleeing to western Guizhou. The bandit forces are scattered and can be easily annihilated. (Central News Agency dispatch, 16th)

New Security Force: Replacement Delayed by Several Days, Two Brigade Commanders Arrive in Beiping to Meet with He, War Zone Clearing Committee to Extend Three Months Before Conclusion 6

(Beiping) The War Zone Clearing Committee has not yet completed all the outstanding issues in the war zone. The committee was originally scheduled to be established for six months, but it is now rumored that it will be extended by three months to continue handling the clearing affairs in the war zone. The replacement of the newly formed security force has been delayed until the end of this month because the defense area has not been demarcated, the command authority has not been determined, and the headquarters of the first and second brigades have not yet found suitable housing. Zhang Yantian and Zhang Qingyu, the commanders of the security brigades, came to Beiping yesterday to meet with Yin Rugeng and then, accompanied by Yin, met with He to report on the inspection and downsizing of the security force. They also went to the Political Reorganization Council to meet with Wang Kemin. (Special dispatch, 17th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng stated that the new security force's entry into the war zone for replacement has not yet been properly arranged due to housing and transportation issues, and the departure date has not yet been determined. The allocation of police force in each county and the number of security forces stationed in each county will be determined after they enter the area. The old security team of Fan Jinghua has been transferred to the outskirts of Beiping for training and will return to the team after reorganization. Zhou Yuying's troops are currently stationed in Yutian to handle rural clearing. After the rural clearing is completed, they will be withdrawn. The reorganization of Li Yuansheng's troops stationed in the Yanjiao Xiadian area will be carried out as soon as the provincial government issues the reorganization funds. The establishment of a security command in the war zone has precedents in the southern provinces that can be followed. Yin will go south to negotiate this matter. He does not plan to leave Beiping recently. (Special dispatch, 17th)

Rampant Spread of Secret Societies in Various Counties of Southern Hebei, Inciting Salt Workers to Attempt Riots, Tax Police Still Stationed in Nanle County Seat 9

(Tianjin) In Nanle County, Southern Hebei, 12 branches of the Xingyi Dadao (Big Sword) Society gathered 4,000 people and surrounded the county seat, demanding that the tax police stationed in the Eighth District withdraw from the area. The tax police left the city in the afternoon and clashed with the members of the society, resulting in a fierce battle lasting three hours. One tax policeman was killed and two were injured, while three members of the society were killed and countless were injured. In Daming, Qingfeng, Qutong and other areas, secret societies such as the Red Spears and Yellow Sand societies took the opportunity to incite the salt workers and issue absurd leaflets, attempting to riot. The situation is extremely tense. On the afternoon of the 12th, Zhang Yongheng, the magistrate of Nanle County, Wang Haifeng, the magistrate of Qingfeng County, and gentry from Nanle negotiated and persuaded the members of the Big Sword Society and the tax police to temporarily cease hostilities. It was also mediated that the tax police would remain stationed in the Nanle county seat, and the salt workers would be temporarily allowed to scrape the leaching saltpeter. However, the secret societies and salt workers gathered in increasing numbers, agreeing to pay two yuan per salt worker to the secret societies for supplies, thoroughly resisting the tax police. (Special dispatch, 17th)

(Tianjin) After the Nanle conflict, the salt workers in Qutong, Handan, Jize, Pingxiang, and the bordering areas of Henan's Neihuang, Hua County, Fan County, and Shouchang were all restless. Secret societies in various places took the opportunity to expand their influence, and the people were quite panicked. (Special dispatch, 17th)

(Tianjin) The Hebei County Party Headquarters telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Party Headquarters to report that there are over 70 counties in Southern Hebei that produce leaching saltpeter. Due to the infertile land and the unsuitability for cultivation, hundreds of thousands of people rely on leaching saltpeter for their livelihood. If it is completely banned, millions of people will have no way to make a living, and the barren land will be turned into wasteland. It is expected that they will take risks and cause incidents. The Party Headquarters also suggested six measures: establishing a loan institution for the people to enable them to change their profession and provide spring farming assistance, establishing agricultural loan societies, exempting taxes, and requesting the Changlu salt transport envoy to handle the matter. Current Commentary

Dumping of Foreign Cigarettes and the Domestic Cigarette Industry 24

— Yan

Since the cigarette consolidated tax was changed to a two-tier tax system, the domestic Chinese cigarette industry has had to compete among themselves because of the heavy tax rates, coupled with the bankruptcy of the rural areas and the reduction in purchasing power. On the one hand, they have tried to reduce prices to attract customers. On the other hand, they have also included huge bonuses and gifts (the so-called "gift cigarettes") to entice customers. Their willingness to make a desperate bet is nothing more than to seek self-preservation and to strive to survive with all their might. However, since the popularity of this "gift cigarette," the sales of domestic cigarettes have indeed increased sharply. However, in terms of sales volume, the total sales for the whole year last year were only more than 400,000 cases, only half of what it was in previous years. Therefore, most manufacturers have found that profits are meager and losses are huge. Those who can obtain slightly better business records are few and far between.

Now, since March of this year, the production of "gift cigarettes" has been banned. Moreover, starting next month, the sale of these "gift cigarettes" will also be prohibited. Since the order was issued, the sales of domestic cigarettes have plummeted and prices have fallen sharply. At the same time, the cigarettes of British and American companies have taken the opportunity to dump their products on the market. According to statistics, the output of British and American tobacco companies was only more than 10,000 cases per month in the least prosperous times. In recent months, sales have increased by approximately 36,000 cases per month. It is estimated that monthly sales will reach a huge 50,000 cases. Moreover, their selling prices have been drastically reduced in order to compete. For example, the "Little Fairy" brand used to sell for more than 160 yuan per case, but now it only sells for 142 yuan. Moreover, each empty pack can be exchanged for one cigarette, which requires a reduction of approximately 14 yuan. That is, each case is actually sold for 128 yuan. After deducting the consolidated tax of 80 yuan, there are still 48 yuan left. After deducting the cost of raw materials, wages, discounts, and commissions, it is actually feared that it is not enough to cover the cost. Such competition is hardly easy for our Chinese cigarette industry, which has weak capital, to resist.

The reason why British and American tobacco companies are making huge sacrifices and eagerly taking this action is nothing more than relying on their strong capital to overwhelm the Chinese cigarette industry in order to dominate the Chinese market forever. Therefore, starting on November 1, last year, they specially reorganized the original British-owned British American Tobacco Company in China, the British Great Britain Tobacco Company, and the British Ho Tai Tobacco Co., Ltd. into the British Yizhong Tobacco Co., Ltd. and the British Yizhong Tobacco Sales Co., Ltd. The purpose of the reorganization is to increase efficiency in their business operations and to achieve the effect of division of labor and cooperation in production and sales. Recently, the rights of the Greater American Tobacco Company's manager in China have also been acquired by the company. Their power will become increasingly inflated, and the domestic cigarette industry will be even more seriously affected.

Moreover, British and American tobacco companies not only use their strong capital to oppress our domestic manufacturers, but also use other means to cause various intangible damages to our domestic manufacturers. Fortunately, whenever domestic manufacturers encounter foreign oppression, they often adopt conservative policies to temporarily avoid their edge. Once the oppression is slightly relaxed, they rise up again. Therefore, although they have suffered various difficulties for more than ten years, a small number of manufacturers have still been able to support themselves. However, the number of those who have sacrificed in this process is unknown. Recently, we have once again witnessed the domestic cigarette industry in a difficult situation, unable to recover on its own, and we cannot help but feel deeply moved. We sincerely hope that the government authorities will understand the difficulties of business and the importance of supporting our national industry, and on the one hand, find ways to curb unfair competition from foreign merchants, and on the other hand, provide our domestic manufacturers with considerable assistance and convenience so that the vitality of our domestic cigarette industry will not be completely destroyed by the various strategies of foreign merchants competing against us.

France, England, Italy's Proposal Regarding Germany Passed by the League of Nations Council; Denmark Alone Did Not Vote; Legal Experts Committee Appointed to Study Future Sanctions 25

(Geneva) Today, the League of Nations Council enthusiastically passed the resolution proposed by France, England, and Italy condemning Germany's violation of the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles. Denmark alone did not vote. This ends Germany's hopes of rejoining the League of Nations, and it will increasingly pursue a path of acting unilaterally. However, the resolution of the three countries maintains a peaceful tone and has clear provisions for continued negotiations, so observers still believe that the situation is delicate and there is still room for maneuver. The League of Nations Council meeting today adjourned at 1:25 PM, but will reconvene at 4:30 PM to appoint a committee of legal experts to study economic and financial sanctions to punish those who violate treaties in the future. (National Telegram, 17th)

(Geneva) Today, the League of Nations Council met in a tense atmosphere. French Foreign Minister Laval, on behalf of the governments of Britain, Italy, and France, presented a resolution condemning Germany's violation of the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles and requesting the League of Nations to exercise its autonomous fairness and authority. British Foreign Secretary Simon and Italian representative Aloisi successively spoke in support of France. The meeting was adjourned until tomorrow. The Danish representative said that he must consult with his government and will only be able to express his opinion tomorrow. It is expected that the resolution will be passed without amendment.

Today's Council meeting was the first since Japan withdrew from the League of Nations. Japan's seat had been vacant for two years and has now been removed. Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov was already seated to the left of British Foreign Secretary Simon. When French Foreign Minister Laval presented the resolution, he stated that Germany's unilateral implementation of compulsory military service on March 16 must be condemned. We must now find ways to make the League of Nations Covenant more effective in the collective security organization. The Council is entrusted with maintaining peace and must fulfill its responsibility. France has shown its willingness to pursue peace through its actions. The negotiations that began in London on February 3 have been undermined by Germany's actions. France's policy is not to antagonize any country; the security that France seeks is to be extended to all countries.

Simon spoke after Laval, clarifying that the main aim of the policy outlined in the resolution is to establish collective maintenance of peace within the League of Nations framework and asked everyone to pass this resolution to prove that the League of Nations is united for the principles on which it was founded. If this resolution is passed, the door to universal compromise will remain open.

Aloisi spoke, saying that Italy has always advocated revising the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles, but it must be done legally through negotiations.

Polish representative Beck asked whether new sanctions would be proposed to increase the authority of the League of Nations. Polish public opinion is now very concerned that the proposed new coordination may damage the state of peace in northeastern Europe created by Poland concluding the agreement. (Reuters, 16th)

(Geneva) According to informed sources, the League of Nations Council may close today, as Foreign Secretary Simon has indicated that he will leave Geneva this evening no matter what. All parties believe that the draft resolution proposed yesterday will not be amended. If there are any amendments, they will be included in an addendum. (National Telegram, 17th)

Full Text of the Resolution: Unilateral Abrogation of Treaties Harms International Security; Realistic Negotiations and Future Sanctions 26

(Geneva) The full text of the draft resolution submitted by French Foreign Minister Laval to the League of Nations Council on behalf of France, Britain, and Italy is as follows:

According to the opinion of the League of Nations Council:

1. Compliance with all treaty obligations is the fundamental rule of international life and an important condition for maintaining peace.

2. A major principle of human rights is that no country may, without the permission of other contracting parties, abolish obligations in a treaty or change its provisions.

3. The German Defense Law passed on March 16, 1935, is in conflict with these principles.

4. Such unilateral action can never acquire rights.

5. Such unilateral action adds a new source of international chaos and will threaten the security of Europe.

6. Britain and France, with the consent of Italy, have been negotiating with Germany since February 3, 1935, to seek security for all of Europe and to establish universal disarmament based on the principle of Germany's active participation in the League of Nations.

7. Germany's unilateral action is not only inconsistent with this plan, but also occurs precisely when negotiations are underway.

Based on these facts, the League of Nations Council declares:

1. Germany's failure to comply with the treaty has undermined the obligations that the entire international community should bear. The Council condemns such unilateral abrogation of international obligations.

2. The Council requests that the governments that drafted and signed the plan of February 3, 1935, continue these negotiations that have already begun and seek their success within the scope of the League of Nations, and strive to achieve the goals of security, tranquility, and peace.

3. Since the unilateral abrogation of international obligations endangers the existence of the League of Nations, and since the League of Nations' mission is to maintain peace, the Council resolves that such unilateral abrogation of treaties must be subject to the implementation of various necessary measures to protect the security of the people of all countries and European peace. The Council therefore entrusts a committee to propose ways for the League of Nations to maintain peace and to stipulate what special economic and financial measures the League of Nations should take in the future when a member state or non-member state of the League of Nations unilaterally disrupts peace. (National Telegram, 17th)

Statement of the Danish Representative 27

(Geneva) Danish representative Munch stated that he agreed with the constructive parts of the resolution proposed by the French Foreign Minister, but did not agree with condemning the already past violations of the Treaty of Versailles, because once condemned, the work of reconciliation would be hindered, so he did not want to vote. (Reuters, 17th)

Two Stray Bullets in Geneva: Soviet Russia Argues that Sanctions Should Not Be Limited to Europe; Turkey Demands the Liberation of the Dardanelles Strait 28

(Geneva) Just as the Council was about to vote, Litvinov suddenly raised an important reservation of Soviet Russia regarding the French resolution, stating that although Soviet Russia voted in favor of the proposal, it advocated that the condemnation of the unilateral abrogation of treaty obligations should be applied to other continents as well, and should be the same as for Europe. These remarks were clearly directed at Japan's actions in the Far East. For a moment, the representatives of the other powers were all uneasy. British Foreign Secretary Simon immediately asked Litvinov to withdraw his reservation, and Laval and Aloisi also spoke in favor of this. Litvinov finally withdrew at everyone's request, and then the crowd laughed and were relieved.

Today, the Turkish representative suddenly unexpectedly raised the issue of the Dardanelles Strait in the meeting, stating that in the event of any changes to the current situation stipulated in the Treaty of Neuilly, Turkey would have to demand that the military clauses of the treaty regarding the Dardanelles Strait be revised in order to protect Turkey's natural defense line and enjoy equal treatment. Simon immediately stood up and replied, "At present, all I can say is that I will make all reservations." Aloisi and Laval both agreed with Simon's proposal, while Litvinov said that he had no objection to Turkey's aspirations. (Reuters, 17th)

Detailed Report of the League of Nations Meeting: Poland Disagrees with the Three-Nation Proposal 29

(The League of Nations Council meeting in Geneva opened at 11:30 this morning to continue discussions on Germany's violation of the treaty by rearming. As a result of the discussion, the draft resolution of France, Britain, and Italy was unanimously passed by the representatives of the thirteen countries attending the Council: Britain, France, Italy, Russia, Poland, Czechoslovakia, Portugal, Spain, Turkey, Chile, Argentina, Australia, and Mexico. Only Denmark abstained. This morning's meeting was still chaired by Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü. The representatives of the countries that had not expressed their positions at yesterday's meeting had all received instructions from their respective governments today. The first speaker was Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov, who stated that "Germany's notification of withdrawal from the League of Nations has not yet reached the two-year deadline, so it is still a member of the League of Nations. The decision taken by the German government on March 16 violates international treaties. The Soviet government believes that all countries should have equal rights to protect their national security, but the establishment of military equipment should be conditional on being solely for defense purposes. Although Russia did not sign the Treaty of Versailles, it deeply desires to create an international order to prevent any actions that violate treaties." Portuguese representative de Mello Franco then spoke, supporting the draft resolution, saying that "if actions that violate treaties can only be morally condemned, then international order will not be able to progress. Countries that violate treaties should be excluded from the international community. As for countries that have withdrawn from the League of Nations, it is our wish that they can rejoin the League of Nations, but it should be conditional on participating in collective security organizations." Next, Australian representative Bruce spoke, also expressing his support for the draft resolution, hoping that it would be unanimously passed by the Council, and saying that if the League of Nations' actions were to fail, then the member states would only have to take their own steps to ensure security. Spanish representative Madariaga then spoke, saying that "the Council must have moral strength, and the Spanish government will vote in favor of the draft resolution, as it believes that law is more important than power." The representatives of Mexico, Argentina, and Chile spoke one after another, with the same general idea, advocating for unconditional acceptance of the draft resolution. However, Danish representative Munch said, "The Danish government agrees with the various parts of the draft resolution that are not related to Germany, but is deeply afraid that the policy of judging Germany may hinder the success of future negotiations. If the three countries that participated in the Stresa Conference, Britain, France, and Italy, are willing to change the wording of the resolution, then the Danish government is willing to cast a vote in favor; otherwise, the Danish government will abstain." At that point, Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü temporarily relinquished his position as chairman and spoke in his capacity as the Turkish government representative, raising the issue of the demilitarization of the Dardanelles Strait, but stated that this issue would not be discussed at today's meeting. British Foreign Secretary Simon then spoke, making all reservations regarding this issue of Turkey. French Foreign Minister Laval then explained on behalf of Turkey, saying that the Turkish government did not explicitly raise this issue, but only expressed Turkey's desire to join the future collective security system in the Balkans. Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov then declared that there would be no difficulty in realizing this wish of Turkey. At that point, the draft resolution was put to a vote and unanimously passed. The Council meeting was adjourned at 1:00 PM. (Havas, 17th)

(Geneva) The Spanish representative said that he could not abstain from voting in favor of guaranteeing that justice prevails over might. Australian representative Bruce said that general public opinion believes that the world's peace status has already deteriorated, and Australians are particularly uneasy about this. The fear of security has now been crystallized by Germany's unilateral actions, forcing them to deal with the crisis. He believes that the Council's unanimous vote in favor will build a road for cooperation with European countries within the League of Nations and formulate an agreement to guarantee world peace and security. (Reuters, 17th)

(Geneva) This afternoon, the League of Nations Council met, and the representatives of France, Britain, and Italy jointly presented a draft resolution opposing Germany's unilateral abrogation of the treaty and rearmament. The representatives of the countries attending the Council then expressed their opinions one after another. A detailed record of the debate is as follows: When the Council meeting opened this afternoon, French Foreign Minister Laval immediately read a declaration requesting the Council to oppose the German government's decision on March 16, stating that "the Council has a responsibility to maintain peace, and at this time, it is not appropriate to be content with silence or ignore it. The people of all countries know that respecting oaths and keeping the commitments already made are not only a moral principle, but also the golden rule upon which the League of Nations relies for its survival. The countries are following the London Declaration of February 3 and conducting negotiations on the security organization. Germany suddenly announced its rearmament, which makes all negotiations a waste of effort, and people around the world are disappointed and uneasy about it. We do not have any differences of opinion between countries, and all nations should be treated equally. Our policy is not to oppose any other country. The security we demand is not solely for our own purposes, but is intended to make all countries secure. Therefore, although France is submitting this application today, it has never abandoned its commitment to peace. The French government will never hinder any undertakings necessary to achieve understanding among nations. In order to satisfy the requirements of international morality, if adjudicating past events is helpful to overcoming difficulties, then at the same time, the work of the peace organization must never be interrupted, as the work of the peace organization is difficult, circuitous, and difficult to achieve quickly."

After Laval finished his speech, British Foreign Secretary Simon spoke, stating that "the British government, together with the governments of France and Italy, has jointly presented a draft resolution, hoping that this draft will be unanimously passed by the Council. As for the reasons why the three countries, Britain, France, and Italy, have presented this draft resolution, it is based on the final declaration of the Stresa Conference. According to this declaration, the governments of Britain, France, and Italy have decided that when there is a unilateral abrogation of treaty obligations that is sufficient to undermine peace, various methods should be adopted to deal with it jointly. The draft resolution submitted to the Council this time is to expand this obligation of Britain, France, and Italy, and have all member states participate in it. Although this draft resolution is produced by the treaty-breaking action of one country, we can apply it to all countries to achieve the benefits of maintaining peace, and the various items recommended in the draft resolution do not block the door to future negotiations."

Next, Italian representative Aloisi delivered a declaration, stating that "Italy's policy is based on recognizing the actual situation and recognizing the rights and interests of all countries, but anything that is sufficient to undermine European security and peace, such as the unilateral abrogation of the Treaty of Versailles, cannot be supported by Italy. Italy expresses its agreement with the opinions expressed by the representatives of Britain and France. Italy believes that the treaty can be amended, but it must be done through legal channels."

At that point, Polish Foreign Minister Beck spoke, stating that "the Polish government has reservations regarding the following items: (1) the draft resolution on opposing Germany's rearmament; (2) the proposal to strengthen the actions of the League of Nations in the event of any future events that violate treaty obligations, as the Polish government is not inclined to believe in increasing the clauses of the League of Nations Covenant, increasing the constraints on the member states, and enhancing the authority of the Covenant to make the League of Nations more effective; (3) the proposal to conclude another treaty to increase security." Beck also said, "Poland has separately concluded non-aggression treaties with its two neighboring countries, Russia and Germany, making Poland's international relations stable. Now, some people have repeatedly requested finding ways to seek peace in Eastern Europe, so Polish public opinion is unsettled, and Polish public opinion is deeply concerned that the state of peace established by sincere and faithful policies may be damaged by the various proposed new agreements."

Czech Foreign Minister Beneš followed Beck with a speech, generally saying that the Czech government supported the draft resolution presented by Britain, France, and Italy. Spanish representative Madariaga said, "The issue presented today and the procedures adopted are of an extraordinary nature, so it is advocated that the freedom of the Council to discuss this issue should be respected, and if necessary, it should be free to amend the draft resolution." Finally, Danish representative Munch spoke, saying that "the Danish representative expressed agreement with some points in the draft resolution, but requested consultation with his home government before expressing his opinion." At that point, the Council meeting was adjourned and scheduled to continue the discussion at the meeting tomorrow morning. (Havas, 16th)

(Berlin) The Berlin semi-official side released the following message after Polish Foreign Minister Beck made a strong statement in the League of Nations Council: (1) Poland has expressed its attitude towards Germany's rearmament and does not want to express it again. (2) Poland believes that the matter of expanding the responsibilities of the member states of the League of Nations is not within the authority of the Council and should be resolved by the General Assembly. (3) Poland's foreign policy is different from the construction of itself and the policies of Western Europe. Poland's policy takes the maintenance of peace in Eastern Europe as an element. For this reason, Poland has separately established non-aggression pacts with Soviet Russia and Germany. Polish public opinion is deeply concerned that the agreements currently planned may hinder peace in Eastern Europe. All parties attach great importance to the words of Foreign Minister Beck, believing that they represent Poland's attitude towards Europe. (National Telegram, 17th)

Germany Issues Warning: If the Three-Nation Resolution Is Passed, Germany Will Never Return to the League of Nations 30

(Berlin) If the countries of the world adopt the resolutions of the Stresa Conference, then Germany under the rule of the National Socialist Party will never return to the League of Nations. The German government will take an independent attitude, that is, if Germany is discriminated against by other countries, it must have greater military power. This warning was issued by a spokesman for German leader Hitler. As for France's attitude, it is also to be expected, as the French authorities do not hope for the cooperation of the National Socialist Party leader. French Foreign Minister Laval once said that it is Germany, not France, that is being judged by the countries of the world. Germany's blatant violation of the Treaty of Versailles cannot be tolerated by the signatory countries, especially the states neighboring Germany must oppose it. A French spokesman said that France will continue to increase its land and air military strength in order to have sufficient "self-defense" power to prepare for war. Fair observers predict that this action by France will cause an unlimited arms race, because if Germany and France increase their military power, then other countries will also rise up and follow suit, competing for self-defense. If this continues, it will inevitably lead to a situation that is difficult to reverse. (National Telegram, 17th)

(Berlin) The German newspapers this morning unanimously refuted the three-nation proposal submitted to the League of Nations Council yesterday condemning Germany's rearmament, believing that if this proposal is passed, the organization of peace in Europe will be seriously harmed. If the League of Nations arrogantly believes that it has the right to arbitrarily judge defeated Germany, then it will be difficult for Germany to return to the League of Nations. The Berlin Morning Post stated that this proposal is a crime that endangers European peace and will close the door to negotiations with Germany. The Berlin Daily News stated that the three countries not only regard themselves as prosecutors, but also as judges, wanting to determine that Germany is guilty. This kind of action cannot be without serious consequences. (Reuters, 17th)

Direct Franco-German Negotiations: Laval May Meet Hitler 31

(Paris) French and German diplomats may soon be able to resolve their deep-seated centuries-old hatred at the conference table, surrounded by cigar ash. French Foreign Minister Laval and German leader Hitler have long planned to meet, but the situation has become bleak again due to the re-emergence of open conflict in Geneva. However, according to international observers today, it is almost certain that the French Foreign Minister will get off the train and linger in Berlin on his way back from Russia. The meeting between Laval and Hitler will of course be of an informal nature, and the two will only sit with other leaders of the National Socialist Party and talk about all kinds of disputes that could cause a European war. Britain and Italy have no expectations for the Franco-German leaders' meeting, as they believe that there is little chance of a genuine compromise between the two countries. The recent failed talks between Hitler and British Foreign Secretary Simon can serve as a warning. Some people even believe that Hitler's provocative attitude may deepen the resentment between the two countries, and the opportunity for resentment to arise is even greater if he talks about whether the German air force is now equal to Britain's or whether it will be equal to Britain's in the future. France is the country that openly opposes Germany's rearmament most strongly and advocates economic sanctions to punish Germany in the League of Nations. In other words, the meeting between Laval and Hitler is nothing more than an irresistible force encountering an unbreakable material. (National Telegram, 17th)

MacDonald Reports to British Parliament on the Results of the Conference; No Forgiveness for Germany; No New Restrictions on Austria 33

(London) British Prime Minister MacDonald reported to the House of Commons today on the results of the Stresa Conference, saying that we have not forgiven Germany's action of reintroducing compulsory military service, and we have declared that we regard this as a major cause of unrest and a blow to the international peace organization. He continued that Britain has always paid close and friendly attention to the Eastern European Convention and the issue of Austrian independence, but Britain has not undertaken new restrictions and will only consult with other countries when Austrian integrity and independence are endangered. The three countries, Britain, France, and Italy, have agreed to actively study the Western European Air Convention. Italy and Britain have clarified their obligations under the Locarno Treaty. MacDonald mentioned Germany's reintroduction of compulsory military service and said that we have always opened the door to allow Germany to join the movement to create a European collective security system. Our policy will still be based on the League of Nations Covenant. The three countries that participated in the Stresa Conference do not go their separate ways, but will work together as one to find a peaceful solution to today's crisis and cooperate with countries that are willing to join this work. (Reuters, 17th)

The newly established department will begin operations at the beginning of next month. Its first important task is to issue a notice to local officials, detailing the government's policies and how local officials should cooperate with the government, and then issue guidance to the public on how to prepare. German Trade Surplus 41

(Berlin) In March of this year, Germany's foreign trade had a surplus of 12 million marks over imports. This is the first time since last November that there has been such a surplus. The figures released today clearly show that the result of this surplus is encouraging for the future. Several months ago, a large amount of raw materials was imported after many agreements were made with foreign countries to barter goods for goods, and now they can be manufactured and re-exported as raw material exchanges. This observation is based on facts. The amount of imports in March was 353 million marks, lower than the 259 million in February. As for the amount of exports in March, it was 365 million marks, which is a significant increase from the 302 million in February. From this, it can be said that the export trade volume has almost completely improved suddenly. In March 1934, the import amount was 398 million, and the export amount in the same month was 401 million. Therefore, last year's foreign trade was too low. However, compared with the monthly average for the whole year of 1934, the 353 (million marks) in March 1935 has fallen from the average of 371 (million marks). On the contrary, the average export volume in 1934 was 347 (million marks), and in March of the third year of 1935, it rose to 365 (million marks). This proves its actual progress. However, in practice, these two figures still need to be corrected to some extent, because in March 1935, Saar was included in Germany for the first time, and its imports and exports will naturally increase compared to before its return. However, the most relevant figure in Germany's foreign trade at present is the display of its economic and financial probable ability in the world market. This kind of distinction is only a matter of routine relationship. The noteworthy items in the imports in March are the increase in the purchase of wool by 5.2 million marks, timber by 2.2, rubber by 1.9, and mineral oil by 0.6 million marks. These are the raw materials needed for Germany's economic recovery. In addition to Europe, the cotton and metal industries in the United States and the cotton industry in Egypt have increased. The import of Australian wool and Turkish textile raw materials has decreased. (National Press, 16th)

Japan Opposes Russian and German Participation in Naval Conference, Anglo-German Negotiations Proceed Smoothly 42

(Tokyo) It is reported that the British government has decided to hold technical preliminary negotiations with the Soviet Union and Germany in parallel with the disarmament conference to be held this year. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not received any official telegrams. However, the general opinion within the ministry is as follows: (1) The formal arms conference to be held this year is based on the provisions of the Washington Treaty and the London Treaty. Therefore, the participating countries are naturally limited to the five countries of Britain, the United States, France, Italy, and Japan. If the Soviet Union and Germany participate, the disarmament conference will inevitably lead to the same results as the League of Nations general disarmament conference, making the conference even more ineffective. (2) When Germany declared its rearmament last time, the French ambassador to Japan visited Foreign Minister Hirota and requested the participation of the Soviet Union and Germany in the disarmament conference. Foreign Minister Hirota tactfully expressed his opposition at the time, saying that if the Soviet Union and Germany participated, it should be another conference with the Washington Treaty disarmament conference. The empire still adheres to this policy and has not changed in any way. (3) The Empire's government cannot express its satisfaction with turning the arms reduction conference, which focuses on international peace, into a tool for discussing the maintenance of European peace institutions. (Telegraphic News Agency, 17th)

(Washington) Sandstorms are raging, drought is occurring, and the cotton processing tax is unpopular. (Xuzhou) Xiao County is proceeding with the land reporting very quickly. The Xiao and Tong public security teams then launched an attack, resulting in several casualties. International Commerce —Reuter's Special Telegram, April 17th— 66

Gold and Silver: London gold price today is 143 shillings and 4 pence, same as yesterday. London silver market today is unstable, the price fell by 0.1875, spot price is 30.75 pence, futures price is 30.875 pence. India sold, China both bought and sold.

Bombay Silver Market: Today stable, spot price is 72 rupees 4 annas, down 1 anna.

Exchange Rates: Anglo-American: London foreign exchange market, quiet this morning, price fluctuations were minimal and insignificant. The opening exchange rate for Anglo-American was $4.8575, the same as yesterday's closing price. Later, the US dollar strengthened slightly, causing the price to drop to $4.850625, which is 0.006875 lower than the opening price.

Anglo-French: The opening price was 73.59 francs, the same as yesterday's close. There was very little fluctuation before noon, and only fell by 6 points before noon, to 73.53 francs. This price remained unchanged until the time of dispatch.

New York Cotton: Today (April 17), the New York cotton market opened, prices were slightly lower because there was no new impetus. Later, due to better foreign telegrams and some settlement of accounts, prices tended to strengthen. It is expected that the handling fee issue will have a compromise solution.

Chicago Wheat: Early trading still favored news for those who were short, but the Chicago wheat market opened lower today, with prices tending to decline during the morning session.

Bombay Cotton: Today, Bombay cotton prices initially rose due to general buying interest, but then fell back as bulls closed out positions and European exporters also sold. Later, prices rebounded due to good spot demand and purchases by bull speculators. The market closed quietly. White Lohar cotton for July-August delivery was 231 rupees, up 0.25.

Liverpool Wheat: Today the Liverpool wheat market turned firm. The price for July delivery at 1:00 PM was 5 shillings and 9 pence, up 0.0625.

Liverpool Cotton: The market was also firm today. The price at 1:00 PM was 6.39, up 0.04 points.

Tianjin Hengyuan Yarn Factory Prepares to Resume Production 72

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Hengyuan Yarn Factory is preparing to resume production. A consortium of creditor banks is lending 2 million yuan in working capital and sending people to manage it, collecting monthly interest and repaying debts with the surplus. If it loses everything again, the creditor will seize the assets to offset the debt. The Yuyuan Yarn Factory has recently formed a liquidation committee. The Economic Commission is sending a commissioner from the Cotton Industry Control Association to Tianjin to assess the value and auction off the assets to offset the debt. Another new company will take over the factory's assets and resume operations. The East Asia Development Company is making every effort to buy out the Tianjin yarn factory or operate it under a trusteeship, in order to fulfill its ambition to control the yarn industry in North China. The Tianjin Hengyuan, Yuyuan, Beiyang, Huaxin, and Baocheng factories all owe Japanese debts. Currently, only Beiyang and Huaxin are operating, but they are affected by the dumping of Japanese yarn. Each package of fine yarn produced results in a loss of 10 yuan, and they are all in a state of unsustainability. (Special dispatch from the 17th)

Fake Coarse Weaving Mill in Banbishan Establishes Opium Monopoly Bureau 73

(Tianjin) Banbishan, north of Zunhua, is occupied by the puppet Rehe Province, which has established an opium monopoly bureau, forcing people to grow opium and levying a tax of six yuan per mu. Those who do not grow opium are punished. The puppet tax bureau is also levying extremely heavy taxes. Cattle, sheep, and horses are taxed 5 jiao per head per year. Goods transported by Chinese are taxed more than three times the value of the goods. Grain is not allowed to be transported and sold within the territory, resulting in extremely cheap rice and grain. Residents who previously resisted and rebelled have lost courage and have now abandoned their homes and fled. (Special dispatch from the 17th)
