Shanghai Newspaper Local Supplement - Random Notes on Suicide Incidents Dreamruo

The instability of Shanghai society can be seen from the increasing number of suicide cases. Every day, when reading the local newspapers' social news, you can often find one or two suicide messages that are quite striking. These constantly occurring suicide cases are clearly telling you that at present, many people in Shanghai society are already feeling the hardship of survival and have no choice but to embark on the final journey!

Yesterday, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs released a suicide statistics report for the city in the 23rd year: a total of 2,325 suicide cases throughout the year, including 1,122 men and 1,203 women. The causes of suicide were: verbal disputes were the most common, followed by economic pressure, and then family accidents. Suicide results: a total of 501 deaths, 1,816 rescues, and 8 unknown. Age of suicides: 21 to 30 years old was the most common, totaling 1,141, followed by 31 to 40 years old, totaling 461, and then 20 years old, totaling 438.

According to the report from the Bureau of Social Affairs, the large number of suicide cases in the city last year was unprecedented in previous years. If the year is calculated as 365 days, then on average, more than six suicide incidents occur in the city every day, and one occurs every four hours. This number is really shocking and worthy of attention from those who care about social issues!

The endless emergence of suicide incidents is a negative phenomenon in society. The occurrence of this negative phenomenon is attributed by some to the weakness of individual will, and by others to the oppression of the social environment. However, in our observation, both are causes of suicide cases, and the latter is more important than the former. Therefore, to remedy suicide, one must consider both aspects.

However, today's Shanghai society is an unhealthy and deformed society. Various morbidities exist early on in this society. A person living in this society inevitably faces a terrible threat to their life. Therefore, we believe that suicide cases in this city cannot be reduced at present!

Small Town in a Mining Area Tuoren

The train sped through the jungle, and what jumped into view was a deep valley, surrounded by towering peaks. This is the coal mining area.

The iron wheels of the train slowly and tortuously rolled on the hillside, crossing a small, clear mountain stream where you could see the pebbles below, and then entered the platform shrouded in black coal piles towering on all sides.

The people on the platform were so few that there was no vitality. I was squeezed out of the black carriage in the crowd. Several children doing petty business were calling out their wares on the station with bamboo baskets, but in an instant, everyone dispersed. Several old men carried down the unsold fruits from the city from the carriages, pressed them on their shoulders with disappointment, and walked away behind the rails. The person standing at the station office door waved the green flag and blew a silver whistle. The train, a long string of carriages, wriggled past behind the platform. The military station returned to silence. The children selling food were still sitting on the wooden benches of the platform with sad faces, waiting for the train that would come from the city again in two hours. Walking down the platform and crossing the rails lying on the coal dust, less than a hundred steps away, a small street market unfolded in front.

In this mountain valley filled with coal smoke, surrounded by high peaks, this street market is the only marketplace for the tens of thousands of residents living here. Everything is concentrated on this narrow street.

If in a city, a small shop of less than two hundred rooms lined up like this might still be a quiet place, but here, it appears bustling, with people as crowded as on a prosperous street in a big city, and noisy sounds echoing in every corner.

The road surface, paved with crushed stones, has become a slippery mud road under the trampling of people's feet and the random splashing of wastewater from vendors. There is rarely a clean patch of ground. Although there are only about two hundred houses here, they are arranged so briefly that they do not span more than a few hundred steps from beginning to end, but here, there are all kinds of shops: hotels, restaurants, foreign goods stores, grocery stores, restaurants, teahouses, coal shops, rice shops, bathhouses, everything is complete, as if it were a street in a big city. The pedestrians here, apart from the energetic workers preparing to go to work in the mines and the tired workers returning from work in the mines, are just rural women and children, and no other kind of people can be seen. We are just occasional visitors.

It was already dusk. After traveling from early morning to this time, I already felt mentally tired. A group of people were swallowed by the open door of the hotel.

There were two hotels on this street, and our group had already filled more than a dozen small rooms in one of them. Living in such a hotel is even more depressing than living in a birdcage-like pavilion in the city. However, the tired bodies of travelers feel extraordinarily comfortable lying on the bed, as if entering a world of supreme bliss.

Night, like a black cloth, enveloped the earth. The dim kerosene lamp flickered in the silent heart of the street. A burst of music and women's singing echoed deeply.

"Are there any opera singers here?"

Sitting on the wooden stool at the doorway of the dark hotel, I asked a young servant in the hotel.

"Yes. There are singers and sleepers. There are two brothels here. At night, there are girls singing in the teahouses. You can call them over too, the price is very cheap."

The young servant told me very clearly, as if soliciting business for them, making it very clear.

"There are quite a few tricks here."

"Where? A few years ago, this place was really lively! Business was not only done in this mining area, but people from the villages in front and behind the mountains came here to trade. In recent years, because the harvest in the fields has been bad and the wages of the miners have been reduced too much, this place has become so deserted! Otherwise, it would be even more lively than the city."

The young servant mumbled these words after pursing his lips for a long time. But from his words, one can imagine how prosperous the countryside was a few years ago!

Night Snack Hua Mu

In Shanghai, although there are countless people struggling under the iron wheels of life, unable to get enough to eat during the day, apart from a portion living like in paradise, there are still large groups living in lane houses, eating simple meals, and living ordinary lives. If you belong to this middle class, then you may not be without some leisure. Living this kind of life, although you may not praise Shanghai as a paradise on earth, a world of supreme bliss, at least you are unwilling to leave it under any conditions. There are many places that will make you realize that Shanghai is indeed lovely.

Lane life, of course, has many unsightly elements mixed in, but it also has many characteristics that perfectly and flawlessly satisfy your sense of pleasure. This kind of pleasure, this leisure, is naturally something that the starving people living in thatched huts and the "darlings" living in mansions and apartments cannot appreciate and enjoy.

When the sounds of the city gradually subside at night, the lanes gradually enter a state of sleep. The sounds of clappers from the night snack vendors and the long, quiet, and pure low calls pass by under the windows in a melodious manner. At this time, you may be lying in bed or still savoring your favorite book under the glaring light. Hearing these seductive sounds, a kind of feeling that is both ethereal and rich secretly crawls out from your heart. You will no longer hate and fear that it will disturb your thoughts and sleepiness. You can use familiar and accurate discernment to distinguish what kind of sound is selling what. This is wonton. That is Cantonese-style fish congee...

This peddler passes by, and another comes closer and closer from afar. Listening, counting, cravings surge to the throat, you can no longer read the book, sleepiness flies away, completely losing rational self-control, as if hypnotized. Then, you touch your wallet, your craving soaring, lean against the window and look out, shouting.

—Hey, one bowl!

Or.

—One bowl of fish congee!

Immediately, a humble and cunning response comes back.

—Okay, one bowl of wontons.

On the quiet table, a light, smoky aroma flies up. The fragrance stabs your nose, you leisurely raise two fingers, pinch the spoon, scoop up the stomach-filling delicacy, and send it to your mouth one spoonful at a time. At this time, you will no longer use the crude and chaotic attitude of dining, naturally revealing an elegant demeanor, chewing carefully, savoring deeply. After a while, two lips are沾粘with a thin layer of greasiness, and the bowl is empty. The two角子say goodbye to you. Flew away.

However, rest assured, although the角子have flown away, you will not feel regret. The desire for pleasure has been fully satisfied, there is nothing else to ask for. Wipe your mouth, smoke a cigarette, and you can fall asleep soundly.

If your landlord on the third floor also knows how to enjoy the fun of night snacks, then when a small basket containing a bowl of fragrant佳打passes by your window, another indescribable joy will fill your heart. Like eating Foshan Blind Man's Candy, it is fragrant, sweet, crispy, and flaky. You cannot tell which flavor is particularly good, because he has become your comrade under the same desire. Although the two of you cannot see each other, you have understood each other and are smiling knowingly.

However, this kind of night snack fun also varies in intensity with the seasons. In summer nights, it is usually not very enjoyable. Because the stuffiness of the lane house will still make you sweat even at night. In this mood, you will not think of the passing night snack peddler. The most suitable, of course, is winter and autumn nights.

The Mortal World Yingzi

From the time they first began to understand a little about the world, for some unknown reason, they were sent to Nanshan by their father to become novice monks.

From that time until now, a full seven or eight long years have passed, and they have not seen their parents' faces even once. Therefore, the appearance and demeanor of their parents are simply not imprinted in their childish minds. Therefore, at this time, they felt so lonely and sad, thinking that they were people without fathers, mothers, sisters, or relatives. So sometimes in secret, they often lamented their unfortunate life. In such a lonely time, apart from confiding their heart full of melancholy and sadness to the Buddha Dharma, they had no other way to relieve their sorrow.

They often heard the abbot talk about "the mortal world," and in their hearts, they imagined how dangerous, troubled, filthy, ugly, and full of beasts, poisonous snakes, and demons the human world was. Therefore, although they were currently tormented by the thought of missing their parents, when they thought about the people living in such a "lower world," they felt that they were happier than anyone else. However, how quickly did this happiness disappear in their minds! As they gradually grew older, when the sharp changes in their physiology and the natural demands of human nature erupted, they could not suppress their desires no matter what. Regarding the so-called "unbearable mortal world," they often had all kinds of illusions. Even if they did not want to come to "the human world" to try its flavors, they really wanted to understand what "the mortal world" was all about!

One day, when the elder brother took advantage of the abbot's absence, he asked his younger brother with a questioning tone:

"According to the abbot, the mortal world is empty, illusory, and ugly, but the impression I have recently gotten is not like that! The mortal world also has magnificent pavilions, elegant and exquisite gardens, clear mountains and green waters, and bright spring scenery, everything seems to be no less than on the mountain."

"That's right," the younger brother replied, "The mortal world may not be much different from the mountain, but brother, don't you remember the abbot's words? The worst and filthiest thing over there is the root of all evil, and that is women! With women, the mortal world cannot be compared to the mountain." The younger brother said with great confidence.

"So, women must be hateful animals..." The elder novice monk then looked at the younger novice monk with suspicion, and then he said in a low voice, "But according to my recent observation, it is not like that. Haven't you seen that when those young girls, dressed in red and green clothes, come to the mountain to offer sacrifices to the Buddha and immortals, their gentle and graceful actions, their charming posture, and their affectionate eyes and smooth faces, I don't see much difference from goddesses. I heard that the abbot often secretly goes down the mountain behind our backs to seek pleasure with those women. The abbot recites lofty scriptures, but what occupies his heart is this so-called "filthy mortal world." So I have already developed a bad sense of sin towards the Buddha Dharma. In fact, I think as long as we do not do evil deeds, are not tempted, and maintain our pure hearts, I think everywhere is the same...."

The younger brother only nodded, feeling that the elder novice monk's words were half-believed and half-doubted.

Amateur Mailbox - Legal Rights to Inherit Property

Dear Editor:

I am a shop assistant with little knowledge and can be considered a person without any judgment. Recently, I have encountered a problem that I think is extremely difficult to solve, so I have to trouble you to give me a clear indication.

The facts are as follows: I have an uncle and a father. Both my father and my uncle make a living by teaching in the village, while my uncle went out to do business when he was young and earned a lot of money. He only returned to his hometown in recent years to enjoy his old age. However, although he is already over fifty years old, he does not have a son. Four years ago, he had the intention of making me his heir, but at that time I was still studying outside and don't know why he changed his mind. Later, he made his uncle's son his heir. However, that cousin (uncle's son) is not on the right track and is actually associating with gangsters, often asking my uncle for money to gamble, drink, and prostitute himself, truly doing all kinds of evil. My uncle was extremely angry and kicked him out. My uncle also did not take him in, so he drifted outside and there has been no news of him for more than two years. Recently, my uncle discussed with my father again to make me his adopted son. Of course, we have no objections to this matter, but the problem arises: because my cousin, although he has been expelled, will definitely not give up this property. How should I deal with him in the future if he gets entangled with me? Does he have any legal grounds to sue me? Respectfully, Shen Bin

Editor's Note: Article 1143 of the Inheritance Section of the Civil Code stipulates: "If there are no lineal descendants, a will may be used to designate an heir for all or part of the property, but this shall be in accordance with the provisions regarding special reserved portions." Therefore, Mr. Shen's uncle can, of course, freely designate anyone as the heir to his property. However, because there is a fact of raising the cousin in the past (according to the letter, it seems that the formalities of "withdrawal of inheritance" have not been formally completed), in order to avoid future disputes, Mr. Shen's uncle should quickly go to the court or the county government兼理司法的to file the procedures for "withdrawal of inheritance" (referring to the cousin) and "establishment of inheritance" (referring to Mr. Shen), and at the same time, the will must be prepared; in our opinion, this will should adopt a "notarized will" to be appropriate.

The above is just a way to solve this problem from a legal standpoint. But we believe that enjoying unearned wealth can only cultivate people's habits of pleasure and extravagance, and there is a danger of extinguishing the enterprising spirit of young people, which is not a very gratifying thing. Therefore, if Mr. Shen's uncle insists on making Mr. Shen his heir, in order to make the old man feel comforted, of course, he cannot refuse. But you must never think of this as an opportunity to make a fortune! Mr. Shen's responsibility is to find a way to find his cousin and guide him to the right path. After a person has been greatly stimulated, it is easy to abandon evil and return to goodness. At that time, Mr. Shen should also intercede on his behalf in front of his uncle and restore their relationship. As for the uncle's property, it may be divided equally between the two. This way, he will not disappoint the old man now, and he can take care of the feelings of his brothers, and he will not lose considerable benefits himself: this is the most appropriate and noblest solution.

Finally, because it is not yet known whether Mr. Shen's cousin can be determined to do good, we believe that legal procedures should still be completed as soon as possible, so that the right can be exercised by oneself. This is what is meant by having a complete plan.

Shanghai Newspaper Local Supplement Movie Special Issue "Little Minister" Special Issue The Beginning and End of James Barrie's Famous Work "Little Minister" Being Made into a Movie Xiaosheng

(1) The Popularity After Publication

Sir James Barrie's world-renowned literary masterpiece "Little Minister" is now being brought to the silver screen with sound to satisfy the world's desire. The main character, Babbie, is played by the exceptional and talented actress Kathleen Hepburn.

When he wrote this story about a Gypsy girl and a minister's love story, Barrie never imagined that forty-three years later, this story would be enjoyed by millions of people around the world in a sound movie.

Since its initial publication in 1891, this novel has caused a sensation around the world and has been reprinted repeatedly. Later, the original author also wrote it into a script, which has been made into two silent films. And it is often broadcast on the radio. Now that it has been made into a sound movie, it will undoubtedly cause an even greater sensation and give people a deeper understanding.

In 1891, "Little Minister" was published daily in a London magazine. At the end of the same year, the single-volume edition of "Little Minister" made its first appearance to the world. This vivid, touching, and sorrowful love history immediately became a hit, receiving praise from millions of people. And the background of this novel, the author's hometown, the "Forest" village, has also become a world-renowned scenic spot. At that time, American newspapers published it one after another. According to recent surveys, more than one million copies of "Little Minister" have been sold in the United States alone. The publishing industry is still constantly reprinting it. Moreover, because of RKO's successful production, the sales of this immortal masterpiece have increased extraordinarily.

(2) The Script Conversion Was Equally Successful

Undoubtedly, "Little Minister" can be made into a script. In 1897, the author himself wrote it into a script. At that time, people's enthusiasm for welcoming and praising this script was the same as their enthusiasm for the novel.

Soon, this script was introduced to the Americas and obtained by the then-theatrical king Charles Frohman. After the play was performed, it became a sensation throughout the United States. And Miss Adams, who played the main character in the play, immediately became extremely popular. She performed "Little Minister" continuously on Broadway for as many as three hundred performances. Later, she traveled throughout the United States with "Little Minister." But the people of London did not have the pleasure of seeing "Little Minister" performed at the "Duke of York" theater until 1914. In 1934, Miss Adams broadcast "Little Minister" on New York National Radio. All the way to 1935, Rose Coghlan continued Miss Adams' role in starring in this play in New York. And the script has also been improved a lot.

Setbacks in Silent Film Era Production Feite

In the silent film era, many people were eager to bring "Little Minister" to the silver screen. Vitagraph Company then began to produce this "Little Minister" novel. But after some minor setbacks, the work was stopped.

In 1921, Paramount decided to make it into a movie. As soon as the news leaked, Vitagraph immediately came forward to oppose Paramount's production rights. But Paramount cleverly bought the copyrights of both scripts and secretly went to produce it. This matter was finally known to Vitagraph, and they quickly rushed to produce the "Little Minister" novel day and night. As a result, these two "Little Minister" silent films were performed on the American screen almost simultaneously.

RKO Pictures has now turned this immortal masterpiece of more than forty years into a sound film, with the "Little Women" protagonist Kathleen Hepburn and John Beal collaborating again. When Sir Barrie, the original author of the script, heard this news, he sent a telegram from Scotland to RKO Pictures congratulating them, saying: "I am deeply gratified that your company has such a good actress as Miss Kathleen Hepburn to play the role of Babbie."

The Scenery of Doune Made Her Reluctant to Leave Huimu

During the production of "Little Women," the most burdensome work that RKO Pictures felt was to build a Scottish village of Doune. Doune village was the name of the eighteenth century. It has now been changed to Killinmore village.

With the economic capabilities of a large company in Hollywood, this small Scottish village was actually created in the shade of the mountains of California. It is not only exactly the same as the Scottish rural style, but it is also a truly beautiful work of art. The authors are the general experts in Scottish-style architecture and landscape arrangement.

There is the lovely village of Doune, which is the former residence of Sir James Barrie, the original author of "Little Women." Behind it is the towering Lindores Abbey, which is built according to the ancient Norman-style fortress. The fortress has soaring roofs, stone walls, windows made of stained glass, magnificent iron gates, and towering stone steps.

Returning to the village, there is where the poor weavers live. There is the town hall, the public square, the blacksmith shop, old woman Nan's broken house, the church, and the "Little Minister's" residence.

There are also mountains. There are windmills on the mountains, and crowds of weavers at the foot of the mountains, and watchtowers used for observation, which can be used to raise their arms and shout when soldiers come to attack, and thousands of people will immediately stand up.

Among these many beautiful sceneries, this group of people, led by director Richard Wallace, are filming every day. Kathleen Hepburn, the star of "Little Women," is playing the Little Minister's lover here, wandering in this place every day. After "Little Minister" was finished, she was reluctant to leave. Because after months of getting along with such natural scenery, it has become her hometown.

Kathleen Hepburn, John Beal, and Alan Hale's Performances in "Little Minister"

One of the most touching scenes in "Little Minister." Nan (played by Elsie Gordon), an old woman who is nearing the end of her life, is about to be evicted by the landlord and sent to a nursing home. When Babbie (Kathleen Hepburn) comes, she quickly bears her living expenses and keeps her in her old residence. The old woman is extremely grateful and tearful.

Kathleen Hepburn's Self-Filmed Movie During the Production of "Little Minister" Si Qi

Ms. Kathleen Hepburn now has a huge collection of special and unusual films. This is because it was obtained from the big movie "Little Minister" she starred in.

When "Little Minister" was being produced, she used a handheld camera to film herself. When she was performing, she would ask her friends to film, and she would also ask people to record sound for her own film.

Since she is so happy about making movies, she has her own laboratory and sound movie equipment at home. She collects a special place for the "Little Minister" film, not just an extra set of films. But in the film, she took many actors, extras, herself and her friends, all of whom were taken into it. These are all completely absent from the official film.

On the way back after a disturbance, Babbie meets the Little Minister again. The bell that清越of the expression when they talk under the tree was finally found by them Dong Lu

The gentle and harmonious sound of bells from a small church in a picturesque Scottish place. In order to be authentic, RKO needed to find the sound of this bell to produce "Little Minister."

They tried all kinds of bells, no matter what form or size, but they could not find the bell sound that should be in the Oly little church in "Little Minister."

Mrs. Bessie, the director of the investigation department at RKO Pictures, finally visited Bishop Cantwell of the Catholic Church in Los Angeles and asked him if there was such a bell in the churches under his jurisdiction. As a result, he told Mrs. Bessie that there was such a bell in St. Victor's Church. After testing, they finally found the bell sound they wanted. With the bishop's permission, the sound department asked the bell that had been sought after the ends of the earth to capture its sound.

Silver Screen Tracking Literature "Little Minister" Forever Immortal Liusha

The most popular and enduring novel of the past fifty years—this is Sir James Barrie's immortal literary masterpiece "Little Minister."

Now RKO Pictures has brought this world-famous masterpiece to the screen, starring the talented actress Kathleen Hepburn, who is admired by everyone. According to the observations of people related to the production of this film, the result of this silver screen masterpiece in the future will definitely be as immortal as Sir Barrie's original work.

The RKO Pictures staff have racked their brains to make the progress of this film as expressive as the writing style of the novel. The essence of that immortal masterpiece is dedicated as much as possible to the people who love silver screen art to appreciate.

In addition to Kathleen Hepburn, who plays the main character, and John Beal, who plays the Little Minister, who need no introduction, all the other supporting actors are the best actors of their time.

During the fierce battle between soldiers and villagers, the Gypsy girl Babbie goes wild and assists the villagers to resist the soldiers' previous expression.

A Brief History of Little Minister Male Lead John Beal Chang

Most stage actors, if they want to break into the movie circle, they must go through all kinds of difficulties before they have a place to gain a foothold.

John Beal's situation is not like this. He was hired by Hollywood to star in his famous stage play called "Another Language". After his success, because he refused to sign any contracts with people, he ran back to the stage.

But soon he was strongly invited by RKO Pictures to return to the film city to star in "Wife's Secrets" "Hat, Coat, & Gloves". The success of his performance art made RKO Pictures assign him to co-star with Kathleen Hepburn in the world-famous literary masterpiece "Little Minister" Little Minister. In addition to achieving great success in "Little Minister" with his pure and superb art and his gifted performing talent, he has now signed a contract to make another new film.

Beal is a mixed race of German and Irish descent. His real name is James Alexander Bliedon. It was his first time on stage when he performed drama at a senior high school. Later, at Pennsylvania University, he joined a famous drama club as an actor. His performance skills were appreciated by the New York theater industry.

But the first place he formally performed on stage was the Hedgerow Theatre where Anhartin was trained and successful. He returned to New York and, for a time, completely stopped his stage life and joined a student art union to study. Later, when Frank's famous play "That's Gratiude" was completed, he resumed his stage life and constantly developed his artistic brilliance.

Beal is five feet eleven inches tall. One hundred and eleven pounds in weight. His favorite things in his daily life are ice skating and painting. Swimming and tennis are his favorite sports.

Su Farmer's Bank: Launching Seedling Loans; Expanding Loan Amount by Four Million Yuan; Ordering All Branches to Implement Uniformly 102

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Jiangsu Provincial Farmer's Bank is the only rural relief organization in Jiangsu Province. The bank aims to regulate the rural economy to develop agricultural production. Therefore, since undertaking rural relief work, it has achieved significant results. According to the person in charge of the bank, all business operations are premised on serving rural areas. Thus, the bank can be said to assist farmers from the time of production to the time of harvest and marketing, resolving all production problems. The only thing to pay attention to is the preparation before production, which is seedling loans. General Manager Zhao attaches great importance to this loan program. Therefore, this year, the loan amount has been expanded to four million yuan, in order to achieve widespread relief and benefit every farmer. Currently, in view of the upcoming spring plowing season, the bank has already instructed all branches to start this loan program simultaneously. In order to regulate the use of loans, all loans before the harvest period, with the aim of predicting future production across the country (regardless of agricultural or sideline products), such as fertilizer loans, seed loans, agricultural tool loans, livestock loans, and oil loans, can be included as seedling loans. Regarding the procedures for applying for loans, when applying, borrowers must provide a detailed list of the number of acres cultivated, the types of crops, and the intended use of the loan. After approval by the bank, the principle is to issue physical goods. For example, for fertilizer or seed loans, fertilizer or seeds will be purchased and loaned to farmers, in order to prevent the loan from being used for other purposes. However, borrowers of this type of seedling loan must designate the harvested crops as preparation for repayment. The loan amount should not exceed 50% of the estimated harvest, and so on.

It is more appropriate to raise funds for local public use from local sources. Wuxi: Deadline for Reorganizing Treasury Bonds Committee 106

The county government believes that the treasury bonds in each district of this county have always been jointly managed by the local people who organize a management committee, and the "General Rules for the Management Committee of Treasury Bonds in Each District" were formulated and issued by former County Magistrate Pan. However, over time, the committee has not reorganized in accordance with the regulations for a long time and the use of funds has mostly not been approved. Although it was reorganized once last year, it still failed to fully rectify the situation. Therefore, the "Organizational and Management Regulations for the Treasury Bond Management Committee in Each District" have been specially formulated. Yesterday, each district head was specially instructed to quickly reorganize the original treasury bond management committee in the district completely before May 15th, and to instruct the former management committee to create a roster for handover and deposit the cash that had been embezzled into a designated bank.

Jiangsu Provincial Pawnshop Federation: Telegram Requesting Stamp Duty Exemption for Pawn Tickets 108

The Jiangsu Provincial Pawnshop Federation held a general meeting of member representatives of the province in Suzhou on the 10th of this month. The Wuxi Pawnshop Guild proposed that pawn tickets be exempt from stamp duty. After discussion, it was generally believed that pawn tickets with a loan amount of four yuan or more must be affixed with a one-cent stamp, in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of the current Provisional Regulations on Stamp Duty. However, the newly revised Stamp Duty Law of the Legislative Yuan does not include pawn tickets as a document that should be subject to stamp duty, and its tax rate. This also demonstrates that the relationship between pawnshops and the poor has been considered, therefore, it has been liberally exempted. At this time of rural decline and difficulty in the pawnshop business, it is proposed to request the Ministry of Finance to issue a clear order to exempt the current regulations of Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Duty, which stipulate that pawn tickets must be affixed with a one-cent stamp, in advance, etc. The Pawnshop Federation telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday requesting a prompt exemption in order to provide relief and care for the poor.

Haimen: Tax Police Extort Villagers 112

Near Juxing Town in the Fifth District, four tax police officers stationed in Haifu Town suddenly arrived at the home of Zhang Lao Da, a villager, in the afternoon of the other day. They carried guns and searched the house for more than an hour, only finding a little over ten taels of table salt. They claimed that Zhang was selling smuggled salt and detained Zhang at the team headquarters. They used torture to force a confession and extorted one hundred yuan. After Zhang repeatedly begged, the fine was reduced to sixty-five yuan before he was released. Also, in the home of Lu Jing San, a villager in Hehe Town South Village, the Fifth District, a small amount of table salt was taken from the kitchen by two tax police officers, who claimed that it was smuggled salt. As a result, he was fined over thirty yuan. Now, the people in the district, believing that the tax police are indiscriminately arresting good citizens and illegally extorting them, leaving the lives and property of the people unprotected, have jointly petitioned the county government and the Fourth District Headquarters of the Tax Police to quickly stop this behavior and send personnel to thoroughly investigate and deal with it.

Eighty-Year-Old Woman Dies in Fire 113

In An Dong Township, Fifth District, the mother of Yuan Li Fu, Xue, who is over eighty years old, has had her son, Li Fu, leave to earn a living, not returning for several years. Xue lives alone at home, begging for a living. She is extremely impoverished. Around 7 p.m. yesterday, she was cooking dinner and was careless with fire, causing a fire. Suddenly, flames soared into the sky, unable to be contained. By the time neighbors heard the alarm and rushed to rescue her, it was too late. All two thatched houses were reduced to ashes. Xue was unable to escape and died in the fire, her limbs charred, a tragic sight.

Ningbo: Fire on Warship Street 121

No. 19 Warship Street in Ningbo is a public warehouse established by the Fujian community, with a total of 27 warehouses rented to Yihua Sugar Firm, Huifeng Sugar Firm, Fangjing Wei Longji Longan Shop, Fuji Du Yuan Shop, Xinji Sugar Firm, Longji Sugar Firm, Gongshou Flower Shop, and others as storage facilities. Unexpectedly, at 5:20 p.m. yesterday (14th), a fire suddenly broke out in the public warehouse. Because the cotton, flour, peanuts, and other items stored in the warehouse are easily combustible, and because the northeast wind was strong at the time, the fire intensified and spread uncontrollably. Various water dragons rushed to the scene to put out the fire. It was extinguished only after an hour, but all 27 warehouses were burned down, with total losses exceeding 200,000 yuan. The Ningbo Money Industry Guild Hall is located next to the public warehouse. Fortunately, it was not spread because the water dragons were effectively rescued.

Local News

Ministry of Finance: Clearly Orders Principles for Relieving Industry and Commerce; Stipulates Ten Standards for Loan Issuance 123

The Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will raise 20 million yuan to relieve industry and commerce, of which 15 million yuan will be used for secured loans with collateral, and 5 million yuan will be used for guaranteed loans with credit. Because the Central Bank stipulates that it is not allowed to make mortgage and credit loans, and the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications stipulate that it is not allowed to make credit loans, now, for the purpose of relief, the Ministry of Finance has approved an exception. The Ministry order was issued yesterday. The Ministry order stipulating the standards for relieving industry and commerce is recorded below:

In order to facilitate the relief of industry and commerce, the Ministry has specially strengthened the financial resources of banks and has repeatedly issued separate orders to the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Shanghai Banking Association to discuss and develop concrete measures, and to implement loan issuance as soon as possible in accordance with the banks' articles of association. However, the nature of industrial and commercial firms in Shanghai is different, and the need for loan relief varies. Standards should be clearly defined to facilitate implementation. The principles for loan issuance are specially stipulated as follows: 1. When industry and commerce request loan relief, banks should make every effort to lend in order to maintain the market. 2. Requests for loan relief from industry and commerce are limited to factories that manufacture national goods, merchants that sell national goods, and those that transport national goods for export. 3. When a factory or merchant requests loan relief, the bank should verify whether the factory or merchant actually exists, and carefully investigate its assets and liabilities, profit and loss status, business policy, and whether the requested loan is necessary. 4. The bank should supervise and inspect the use of funds borrowed by factories or merchants at any time, and shall not be used for other purposes. 5. Factories or merchants that have been found to have no ability to continue to exist shall not request a loan. 6. Regarding technical improvements in factories and the business policies of merchants, the bank may send experts to guide or correct them at any time. 7. The monthly interest rate on bank loans to relieve industry and commerce shall not exceed eight li. If the factory or firm's situation cannot afford the full monthly interest, it may request the Ministry to approve a subsidy of two li per month. 8. The repayment period for the foregoing loans shall not exceed one year at the longest. The total amount of loans from each bank shall be limited to 15 million yuan, but after each loan, the bank shall report the details of the number of the loan recipients, the amount, the term, and the collateral to the Ministry for record. 9. For factories or firms that cannot provide collateral and are in urgent need of relief, if there are two reputable merchants who are jointly liable as guarantors for repayment, and the bank approves and requests a small loan, the bank should also provide a loan as appropriate to provide relief, but the total amount of the loan shall not exceed half of the factory or firm's capital and public reserve. The repayment period shall be in accordance with market practice and shall be paid at the end of the period. 10. The total amount of the foregoing credit small loans shall not exceed 5 million yuan in total for each bank loan. The above measures are intended to consolidate finance in the midst of relief, so as to take both into account. This order.

Foreign Banks Do Not Ship Silver Out; Financial Situation Becomes More Stable; No Need to Increase Equalization Tax Rate 124

A reporter from Xin Sheng She learned from foreign banks yesterday morning that all foreign banks, large and small, in Shanghai participated in the meeting of the Foreign Banks Association the other day. Cockburn (Chairman of the Foreign Banks Association), the deputy manager of the Mercantile Bank, first reported the meeting with Song Ziwen and solemnly stated that the Chinese government has decided not to prohibit the export of silver, abolish the silver standard, and reduce the fineness of silver coins. It can be guaranteed by credibility. However, since the overseas silver price is higher than the domestic price, the Chinese government is deeply concerned that silver will flow out again. It hopes that foreign banks will not ship silver out, and cooperate to maintain the market. It was unanimously agreed at the time to temporarily not load silver for export. All foreign banks will abide by it.

No Need to Increase Tax Rate

The equalization tax rate announced by the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee every day at 10 a.m. can be used to cope with the high and low overseas silver prices. However, foreign banks in China have already agreed to temporarily not ship silver out, and customs offices have been ordered to strictly suppress smuggling, which has been quite effective. Moreover, the Chinese people have a deep understanding of the situation and accept the government's advice not to ship silver out. Therefore, China's silver reserves do not flow out due to the overseas silver price being higher than the domestic price. In fact, there is no need to increase the equalization tax rate. Moreover, an increase in the equalization tax will inevitably lead to a tightening of foreign exchange, which will affect the market. Therefore, the equalization tax rate has been the same for several days.

Foreign Exchange Equalization Tax Remains the Same

The equalization tax rate announced at 10 a.m. yesterday was 6.75 percent based on a rate of one shilling ten pence and one two five. As for the exchange rate for telegraphic transfers announced by the Central Bank today, one yuan per pound in London is one shilling seven pence six two five, one hundred yuan per U.S. dollar in New York is thirty-nine dollars six eight seven five, one hundred yuan per franc in Paris is sixty point one francs, and one hundred yuan per mark in Berlin is ninety-eight marks. The exchange rates for London, New York, and Berlin are the same as yesterday, except that the franc in Paris is one franc higher.
